This isn't anything new.

In short, creating a page resource (an image) by setting `content.value` to the string returned by a global resource's `.Content` value results in intermittent errors:

> error calling Resize: failed to resize image "/home/kijana/Code/hugo-forum-topic-54852/content/products/_content.gotmpl": resize /products/window-frame/01.jpg: invalid JPEG format: short Huffman data

But the image is not corrupt in any way (views fine in any app, exiftool likes it, ImageMagick has no complaints, etc.).

```text
rm -rf resources && hugo
```

    50	        // The same template may be executed multiple times for multiple languages.
    51	        // The Store can be used to store state between these invocations.
    52	        Store() *hstore.Scratch
    53	
    54	        // By default, the template will be executed for the language
    55	        // defined by the _content.gotmpl file (e.g. its mount definition).
    56	        // This method can be used to activate the template for all languages.
    57	        // The return value will always be an empty string.
    58	        EnableAllLanguages() string
    59	}
    60	
    61	var _ PagesFromDataTemplateContext = (*pagesFromDataTemplateContext)(nil)
    62	
    63	type pagesFromDataTemplateContext struct {
    64	        p *PagesFromTemplate
    65	}
    66	
    67	func (p *pagesFromDataTemplateContext) toPathSitesMap(v any) (string, map[string]any, map[string]any, error) {
    68	        m, err := hmaps.ToStringMapE(v)
    69	        if err != nil {
    70	                return "", nil, nil, err
    71	        }
    72	
    73	        path, err := cast.ToStringE(m["path"])
    74	        if err != nil {
    75	                return "", nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("invalid path %q", path)
    76	        }
    77	
    78	        sites := hmaps.ToStringMap(m["sites"])
    79	
    80	        return path, sites, m, nil
    81	}
    82	
    83	func (p *pagesFromDataTemplateContext) AddPage(v any) (string, error) {
    84	        path, sites, m, err := p.toPathSitesMap(v)
    85	        if err != nil {
    86	                return "", err
    87	        }
    88	
    89	        hash, hasChanged := p.p.buildState.checkHasChangedAndSetSourceInfo(path, sites, m)
    90	        if !hasChanged {
    91	                return "", nil
    92	        }
    93	
    94	        pe := &pagemeta.PageConfigEarly{
    95	                IsFromContentAdapter: true,
    96	                Frontmatter:          m,
    97	                SourceEntryHash:      hash,
    98	        }
    99	
   100	        // The rest will be handled after the cascade is calculated and applied.
   101	        if err := mapstructure.WeakDecode(pe.Frontmatter, pe); err != nil {
   102	                err = fmt.Errorf("failed to decode page map: %w", err)
   103	                return "", err
   104	        }
   105	
   106	        if err := pe.Init(true); err != nil {
   107	                return "", err
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        p.p.buildState.NumPagesAdded++
   111	
   112	        return "", p.p.HandlePage(p.p, pe)
   113	}
   114	
   115	func (p *pagesFromDataTemplateContext) AddResource(v any) (string, error) {
   116	        path, sites, m, err := p.toPathSitesMap(v)
   117	        if err != nil {
   118	                return "", err
   119	        }
   120	
   121	        hash, hasChanged := p.p.buildState.checkHasChangedAndSetSourceInfo(path, sites, m)
   122	        if !hasChanged {
   123	                return "", nil
   124	        }
   125	
   126	        var rd pagemeta.ResourceConfig
   127	        if err := mapstructure.WeakDecode(m, &rd); err != nil {
   128	                return "", err
   129	        }
   130	        rd.ContentAdapterSourceEntryHash = hash
   131	
   132	        p.p.buildState.NumResourcesAdded++
   133	
   134	        if err := rd.Validate(); err != nil {
   135	                return "", err
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        return "", p.p.HandleResource(p.p, &rd)
   139	}
   140	
   141	func (p *pagesFromDataTemplateContext) Site() page.Site {
   142	        return p.p.Site
   143	}
   144	
   145	func (p *pagesFromDataTemplateContext) Store() *hstore.Scratch {
   146	        return p.p.store
   147	}
   148	
   149	func (p *pagesFromDataTemplateContext) EnableAllLanguages() string {
   150	        p.p.buildState.EnableAllLanguages = true
   151	        return ""
   152	}
   153	
   154	func (p *pagesFromDataTemplateContext) EnableAllDimensions() string {
   155	        p.p.buildState.EnableAllDimensions = true
   156	        return ""
   157	}
   158	
   159	func NewPagesFromTemplate(opts PagesFromTemplateOptions) *PagesFromTemplate {
   160	        return &PagesFromTemplate{
   161	                PagesFromTemplateOptions: opts,
   162	                PagesFromTemplateDeps:    opts.DepsFromSite(opts.Site),
   163	                buildState: &BuildState{
   164	                        sourceInfosCurrent: hmaps.NewCache[string, *sourceInfo](),
   165	                },
   166	                store: hstore.NewScratch(),
   167	        }
   168	}
   169	
   170	type PagesFromTemplateOptions struct {
   171	        Site         page.Site
   172	        DepsFromSite func(page.Site) PagesFromTemplateDeps
   173	
   174	        DependencyManager identity.Manager
   175	
   176	        Watching bool
   177	
   178	        HandlePage     func(pt *PagesFromTemplate, p *pagemeta.PageConfigEarly) error
   179	        HandleResource func(pt *PagesFromTemplate, p *pagemeta.ResourceConfig) error
   180	
   181	        GoTmplFi hugofs.FileMetaInfo
   182	}
   183	
   184	type PagesFromTemplateDeps struct {
   185	        TemplateStore *tplimpl.TemplateStore
   186	}
   187	
   188	var _ resource.Staler = (*PagesFromTemplate)(nil)
   189	
   190	type PagesFromTemplate struct {
   191	        PagesFromTemplateOptions
   192	        PagesFromTemplateDeps
   193	        buildState *BuildState
   194	        store      *hstore.Scratch
   195	}
   196	
   197	func (b *PagesFromTemplate) AddChange(id identity.Identity) {
   198	        b.buildState.ChangedIdentities = append(b.buildState.ChangedIdentities, id)
   199	}
   200	
   201	func (b *PagesFromTemplate) MarkStale() {
   202	        b.buildState.StaleVersion++
   203	}
   204	
   205	func (b *PagesFromTemplate) StaleVersion() uint32 {
   206	        return b.buildState.StaleVersion
   207	}
   208	
   209	type BuildInfo struct {
   210	        NumPagesAdded       uint64
   211	        NumResourcesAdded   uint64
   212	        EnableAllLanguages  bool
   213	        EnableAllDimensions bool
   214	        ChangedIdentities   []identity.Identity
   215	        DeletedPaths        []PathHashes
   216	        Path                *paths.Path
   217	}
   218	
   219	type BuildState struct {
   220	        StaleVersion uint32
   221	
   222	        EnableAllLanguages  bool
   223	        EnableAllDimensions bool
   224	
   225	        // PathHashes deleted in the current build.
   226	        DeletedPaths []PathHashes
   227	
   228	        // Changed identities in the current build.
   229	        ChangedIdentities []identity.Identity
   230	
   231	        NumPagesAdded     uint64
   232	        NumResourcesAdded uint64
   233	
   234	        sourceInfosCurrent  *hmaps.Cache[string, *sourceInfo]
   235	        sourceInfosPrevious *hmaps.Cache[string, *sourceInfo]
   236	}
   237	
   238	func (b *BuildState) hash(v any) uint64 {
   239	        return hashing.HashUint64(v)
   240	}

   238	func (b *BuildState) hash(v any) uint64 {
   239	        return hashing.HashUint64(v)
   240	}
   241	
   242	type sourceInfo struct {
   243	        siteHashes map[uint64]uint64
   244	}
   245	
   246	func (b *BuildState) checkHasChangedAndSetSourceInfo(changedPath string, sites map[string]any, v any) (uint64, bool) {
   247	        hv := b.hash(v)
   248	        hsites := b.hash(sites)
   249	
   250	        si, _ := b.sourceInfosCurrent.GetOrCreate(changedPath, func() (*sourceInfo, error) {
   251	                return &sourceInfo{
   252	                        siteHashes: make(map[uint64]uint64),
   253	                }, nil
   254	        })
   255	
   256	        if h, found := si.siteHashes[hsites]; found && h == hv {
   257	                return hv, false
   258	        }
   259	
   260	        if psi, found := b.sourceInfosPrevious.Get(changedPath); found {
   261	                if h, found := psi.siteHashes[hsites]; found && h == hv {
   262	                        // Not changed.
   263	                        si.siteHashes[hsites] = hv
   264	                        return hv, false
   265	                }
   266	        }
   267	
   268	        // It has changed.
   269	        si.siteHashes[hsites] = hv
   270	        return hv, true
   271	}
   272	
   273	type PathHashes struct {
   274	        Path   string
   275	        Hashes map[uint64]struct{}
   276	}
   277	
   278	func (b *BuildState) resolveDeletedPaths() {
   279	        if b.sourceInfosPrevious == nil {
   280	                b.DeletedPaths = nil
   281	                return
   282	        }
   283	        var pathsHashes []PathHashes
   284	        b.sourceInfosPrevious.ForEeach(func(k string, pv *sourceInfo) bool {
   285	                if cv, found := b.sourceInfosCurrent.Get(k); !found {
   286	                        pathsHashes = append(pathsHashes, PathHashes{Path: k, Hashes: map[uint64]struct{}{}})
   287	                } else {
   288	                        deleted := map[uint64]struct{}{}
   289	                        for k, ph := range pv.siteHashes {
   290	                                ch, found := cv.siteHashes[k]
   291	                                if !found || ch != ph {
   292	                                        deleted[ph] = struct{}{}
   293	                                }
   294	                        }
   295	                        if len(deleted) > 0 {
   296	                                pathsHashes = append(pathsHashes, PathHashes{Path: k, Hashes: deleted})
   297	                        }
   298	                }
   299	                return true
   300	        })
   301	
   302	        b.DeletedPaths = pathsHashes
   303	}
   304	
   305	func (b *BuildState) PrepareNextBuild() {
   306	        b.sourceInfosPrevious = b.sourceInfosCurrent
   307	        b.sourceInfosCurrent = hmaps.NewCache[string, *sourceInfo]()
   308	        b.StaleVersion = 0
   309	        b.DeletedPaths = nil
   310	        b.ChangedIdentities = nil
   311	        b.NumPagesAdded = 0
   312	        b.NumResourcesAdded = 0
   313	}
   314	
   315	func (p PagesFromTemplate) CloneForSite(s page.Site) *PagesFromTemplate {
   316	        // We deliberately make them share the same DependencyManager and Store.
   317	        p.PagesFromTemplateOptions.Site = s
   318	        p.PagesFromTemplateDeps = p.PagesFromTemplateOptions.DepsFromSite(s)
   319	        p.buildState = &BuildState{
   320	                sourceInfosCurrent: hmaps.NewCache[string, *sourceInfo](),
   321	        }
   322	        return &p
   323	}
   324	
   325	func (p PagesFromTemplate) CloneForGoTmpl(fi hugofs.FileMetaInfo) *PagesFromTemplate {
   326	        p.PagesFromTemplateOptions.GoTmplFi = fi
   327	        return &p
   328	}
   329	
   330	func (p *PagesFromTemplate) GetDependencyManagerForScope(scope int) identity.Manager {
   331	        return p.DependencyManager
   332	}
   333	
   334	func (p *PagesFromTemplate) GetDependencyManagerForScopesAll() []identity.Manager {
   335	        return []identity.Manager{p.DependencyManager}
   336	}
   337	
   338	func (p *PagesFromTemplate) Execute(ctx context.Context) (BuildInfo, error) {
   339	        defer func() {
   340	                p.buildState.PrepareNextBuild()
   341	        }()
   342	
   343	        f, err := p.GoTmplFi.Meta().Open()
   344	        if err != nil {
   345	                return BuildInfo{}, err
   346	        }
   347	        defer f.Close()
   348	
   349	        tmpl, err := p.TemplateStore.TextParse(filepath.ToSlash(p.GoTmplFi.Meta().Filename), helpers.ReaderToString(f))
   350	        if err != nil {
   351	                return BuildInfo{}, err
   352	        }
   353	
   354	        data := &pagesFromDataTemplateContext{
   355	                p: p,
   356	        }
   357	
   358	        ctx = tpl.Context.DependencyManagerScopedProvider.Set(ctx, p)
   359	
   360	        if err := p.TemplateStore.ExecuteWithContext(ctx, tmpl, io.Discard, data); err != nil {
   361	                return BuildInfo{}, err
   362	        }
   363	
   364	        if p.Watching {
   365	                p.buildState.resolveDeletedPaths()
   366	        }
   367	
   368	        bi := BuildInfo{
   369	                NumPagesAdded:       p.buildState.NumPagesAdded,
   370	                NumResourcesAdded:   p.buildState.NumResourcesAdded,
   371	                EnableAllLanguages:  p.buildState.EnableAllLanguages,
   372	                EnableAllDimensions: p.buildState.EnableAllDimensions,
   373	                ChangedIdentities:   p.buildState.ChangedIdentities,
   374	                DeletedPaths:        p.buildState.DeletedPaths,
   375	                Path:                p.GoTmplFi.Meta().PathInfo,
   376	        }
   377	
   378	        return bi, nil
   379	}

   431	// Compile sets up the page configuration after all fields have been set.
   432	func (p *PageConfigLate) Compile(e *PageConfigEarly, logger loggers.Logger, outputFormats output.Formats) error {
   433	        if e.IsFromContentAdapter {
   434	                if err := mapstructure.WeakDecode(p.ContentAdapterData, p); err != nil {
   435	                        err = fmt.Errorf("failed to decode page map: %w", err)
   436	                        return err
   437	                }
   438	        }
   439	
   440	        if p.Params == nil {
   441	                p.Params = make(hmaps.Params)
   442	        } else {
   443	                hmaps.PrepareParams(p.Params)
   444	        }
   445	
   446	        if len(p.Outputs) > 0 {
   447	                outFormats, err := outputFormats.GetByNames(p.Outputs...)
   448	                if err != nil {
   449	                        return fmt.Errorf("failed to resolve output formats %v: %w", p.Outputs, err)
   450	                } else {
   451	                        p.ConfiguredOutputFormats = outFormats
   452	                }
   453	        }
   454	
   455	        return nil
   456	}

   458	// MarkupToMediaType converts a markup string to a media type.
   459	func MarkupToMediaType(s string, mediaTypes media.Types) media.Type {
   460	        s = strings.ToLower(s)
   461	        mt, _ := mediaTypes.GetBestMatch(markup.ResolveMarkup(s))
   462	        return mt
   463	}

   486	
   487	func (rc *ResourceConfig) Compile(basePath string, fim hugofs.FileMetaInfo, conf config.AllProvider, mediaTypes media.Types) error {
   488	        if rc.Params != nil {
   489	                hmaps.PrepareParams(rc.Params)
   490	        }
   491	
   492	        // Note that NormalizePathStringBasic will make sure that we don't preserve the unnormalized path.
   493	        // We do that when we create resources from the file system; mostly for backward compatibility,
   494	        // but also because people tend to use use the filename to name their resources (with spaces and all),
   495	        // and this isn't relevant when creating resources from an API where it's easy to add textual meta data.
   496	        rc.Path = paths.NormalizePathStringBasic(path.Join(basePath, rc.Path))
   497	        rc.PathInfo = conf.PathParser().Parse(files.ComponentFolderContent, rc.Path)
   498	        if rc.Content.MediaType != "" {
   499	                var found bool
   500	                rc.ContentMediaType, found = mediaTypes.GetByType(rc.Content.MediaType)
   501	                if !found {
   502	                        return fmt.Errorf("media type %q not found", rc.Content.MediaType)
   503	                }
   504	        }
   505	
   506	        var sitesMatrixFile sitesmatrix.VectorStore
   507	        if fim != nil {
   508	                sitesMatrixFile = fim.Meta().SitesMatrix
   509	        }
   510	
   511	        rc.SitesMatrix = buildSitesMatrixFromSitesConfig(
   512	                conf,
   513	                sitesMatrixFile,
   514	                rc.Sites,
   515	        )
   516	
   517	        rc.SitesComplements = buildSitesComplementsFromSitesConfig(
   518	                conf,
   519	                fim.Meta(),
   520	                rc.Sites,
   521	        )
   522	
   523	        return nil
   524	}

   537	func (s Source) IsZero() bool {
   538	        return !hreflect.IsTruthful(s.Value)

   163	func (r *Spec) NewResourceWrapperFromResourceConfig(rc *pagemeta.ResourceConfig) (resource.Resource, error) {
   164	        content := rc.Content
   165	        switch r := content.Value.(type) {
   166	        case resource.Resource:
   167	                return cloneWithMetadataFromResourceConfigIfNeeded(rc, r), nil
   168	        default:
   169	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to create resource for path %q, expected a resource.Resource, got %T", rc.PathInfo.Path(), content.Value)
   170	        }
   171	}
   172	
   173	// NewResource creates a new Resource from the given ResourceSourceDescriptor.
   174	func (r *Spec) NewResource(rd ResourceSourceDescriptor) (resource.Resource, error) {
   175	        if err := rd.init(r); err != nil {
   176	                return nil, err
   177	        }
   178	
   179	        dir, name := path.Split(rd.TargetPath)
   180	        dir = paths.ToSlashPreserveLeading(dir)
   181	        if dir == "/" {
   182	                dir = ""
   183	        }
   184	        rp := internal.ResourcePaths{
   185	                File:            name,
   186	                Dir:             dir,
   187	                BaseDirTarget:   rd.BasePathTargetPath,
   188	                BaseDirLink:     rd.BasePathRelPermalink,
   189	                TargetBasePaths: rd.TargetBasePaths,
   190	        }
   191	
   192	        isImage := rd.MediaType.MainType == "image"
   193	        var imgFormat images.Format
   194	        var imgOpsSupport images.ImageResourceType
   195	        if isImage {
   196	                imgFormat, imgOpsSupport = images.ImageFormatFromMediaSubType(rd.MediaType.SubType)
   197	        }
   198	
   199	        gr := &genericResource{
   200	                Staler:           &AtomicStaler{},
   201	                h:                &resourceHash{},
   202	                publishInit:      &hsync.OnceMore{},
   203	                keyInit:          &sync.Once{},
   204	                includeHashInKey: isImage,
   205	                paths:            rp,
   206	                spec:             r,
   207	                sd:               rd,
   208	                params:           rd.Params,
   209	                name:             rd.NameOriginal,
   210	                title:            rd.Title,
   211	        }
   212	
   213	        if imgOpsSupport >= images.ImageResourceTypeMetaOnly {
   214	                ir := newImageResource(images.NewImage(imgFormat, r.Imaging, nil, gr), gr)
   215	                return newResourceAdapter(gr.spec, rd.LazyPublish, ir), nil
   216	        }
   217	
   218	        return newResourceAdapter(gr.spec, rd.LazyPublish, gr), nil
   219	}

   185	// should be cached as effectively as possible by the implementation.
   186	type ContentProvider interface {
   187	        // Content returns this resource's content. It will be equivalent to reading the content
   188	        // that RelPermalink points to in the published folder.
   189	        // The return type will be contextual, and should be what you would expect:
   190	        // * Page: template.HTML

   449	func (l *genericResource) Key() string {
   450	        l.keyInit.Do(func() {
   451	                basePath := l.spec.Cfg.BaseURL().BasePathNoTrailingSlash
   452	                if basePath == "" {
   453	                        l.key = l.RelPermalink()
   454	                } else {
   455	                        l.key = strings.TrimPrefix(l.RelPermalink(), basePath)
   456	                }
   457	
   458	                if l.spec.Cfg.IsMultihost() {
   459	                        l.key = l.spec.Lang() + l.key
   460	                }
   461	
   462	                if l.includeHashInKey && !l.sourceFilenameIsHash {
   463	                        l.key += fmt.Sprintf("_%d", l.hash())
   464	                }
   465	        })
   466	
   467	        return l.key
   468	}

    14	// Package hashing provides common hashing utilities.
    15	package hashing
    16	
    17	import (
    18	        "crypto/md5"
    19	        "encoding/hex"
    20	        "io"
    21	        "strconv"
    22	        "sync"
    23	
    24	        "github.com/cespare/xxhash/v2"
    25	        "github.com/gohugoio/hashstructure"
    26	        "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/common/hugio"
    27	        "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/identity"
    28	)
    29	
    30	// XXHashFromReader calculates the xxHash for the given reader.
    31	func XXHashFromReader(r io.Reader) (uint64, int64, error) {
    32	        h := getXxHashReadFrom()
    33	        defer putXxHashReadFrom(h)
    34	
    35	        size, err := io.Copy(h, r)
    36	        if err != nil {
    37	                return 0, 0, err
    38	        }
    39	        return h.Sum64(), size, nil
    40	}
    41	
    42	type Hasher interface {
    43	        io.StringWriter
    44	        io.Writer
    45	        io.ReaderFrom
    46	        Sum64() uint64
    47	}
    48	
    49	type HashCloser interface {
    50	        Hasher
    51	        io.Closer
    52	}
    53	
    54	// XxHasher returns a Hasher that uses xxHash.
    55	// Remember to call Close when done.
    56	func XxHasher() HashCloser {
    57	        h := getXxHashReadFrom()
    58	        return struct {
    59	                Hasher
    60	                io.Closer
    61	        }{
    62	                Hasher: h,
    63	                Closer: hugio.CloserFunc(func() error {
    64	                        putXxHashReadFrom(h)
    65	                        return nil
    66	                }),
    67	        }
    68	}
    69	
    70	// XxHashFromReaderHexEncoded calculates the xxHash for the given reader
    71	// and returns the hash as a hex encoded string.
    72	func XxHashFromReaderHexEncoded(r io.Reader) (string, error) {
    73	        h := getXxHashReadFrom()
    74	        defer putXxHashReadFrom(h)
    75	        _, err := io.Copy(h, r)
    76	        if err != nil {
    77	                return "", err
    78	        }
    79	        hash := h.Sum(nil)
    80	        return hex.EncodeToString(hash), nil
    81	}
    82	
    83	// XXHashFromString calculates the xxHash for the given string.
    84	func XXHashFromString(s string) (uint64, error) {
    85	        h := xxhash.New()
    86	        h.WriteString(s)
    87	        return h.Sum64(), nil
    88	}
    89	
    90	// XxHashFromStringHexEncoded calculates the xxHash for the given strings
    91	// and returns the hash as a hex encoded string.
    92	func XxHashFromStringHexEncoded(s ...string) string {
    93	        h := xxhash.New()
    94	        for _, f := range s {
    95	                h.WriteString(f)
    96	        }
    97	        hash := h.Sum(nil)
    98	        return hex.EncodeToString(hash)
    99	}
   100	
   101	// MD5FromStringHexEncoded returns the MD5 hash of the given string.
   102	func MD5FromStringHexEncoded(f string) string {
   103	        h := md5.New()
   104	        h.Write([]byte(f))
   105	        return hex.EncodeToString(h.Sum(nil))
   106	}
   107	
   108	// HashString returns a hash from the given elements.
   109	// It will panic if the hash cannot be calculated.
   110	// Note that this hash should be used primarily for identity, not for change detection as
   111	// it in the more complex values (e.g. Page) will not hash the full content.
   112	func HashString(vs ...any) string {
   113	        hash := HashUint64(vs...)
   114	        return strconv.FormatUint(hash, 10)
   115	}
   116	
   117	// HashStringHex returns a hash from the given elements as a hex encoded string.
   118	// See HashString for more information.
   119	func HashStringHex(vs ...any) string {
   120	        hash := HashUint64(vs...)
   121	        return strconv.FormatUint(hash, 16)
   122	}
   123	
   124	var hashOptsPool = sync.Pool{
   125	        New: func() any {
   126	                return &hashstructure.HashOptions{
   127	                        Hasher: xxhash.New(),
   128	                }
   129	        },
   130	}
   131	
   132	func getHashOpts() *hashstructure.HashOptions {
   133	        return hashOptsPool.Get().(*hashstructure.HashOptions)
   134	}
   135	
   136	func putHashOpts(opts *hashstructure.HashOptions) {
   137	        opts.Hasher.Reset()
   138	        hashOptsPool.Put(opts)
   139	}
   140	
   141	// HashUint64 returns a hash from the given elements.
   142	// It will panic if the hash cannot be calculated.
   143	// Note that this hash should be used primarily for identity, not for change detection as
   144	// it in the more complex values (e.g. Page) will not hash the full content.
   145	func HashUint64(vs ...any) uint64 {
   146	        var o any
   147	        if len(vs) == 1 {
   148	                o = toHashable(vs[0])
   149	        } else {
   150	                elements := make([]any, len(vs))
   151	                for i, e := range vs {
   152	                        elements[i] = toHashable(e)
   153	                }
   154	                o = elements
   155	        }
   156	
   157	        hash, err := Hash(o)
   158	        if err != nil {
   159	                panic(err)
   160	        }
   161	        return hash
   162	}
   163	
   164	// Hash returns a hash from vs.
   165	func Hash(vs ...any) (uint64, error) {
   166	        hashOpts := getHashOpts()
   167	        defer putHashOpts(hashOpts)
   168	        var v any = vs
   169	        if len(vs) == 1 {
   170	                v = vs[0]
   171	        }
   172	        return hashstructure.Hash(v, hashOpts)
   173	}
   174	
   175	type keyer interface {
   176	        Key() string
   177	}
   178	
   179	// For structs, hashstructure.Hash only works on the exported fields,
   180	// so rewrite the input slice for known identity types.
   181	func toHashable(v any) any {
   182	        switch t := v.(type) {
   183	        case keyer:
   184	                return t.Key()
   185	        case identity.IdentityProvider:
   186	                return t.GetIdentity()
   187	        default:
   188	                return v
   189	        }
   190	}
   191	
   192	type xxhashReadFrom struct {
   193	        buff []byte
   194	        *xxhash.Digest
   195	}
   196	
   197	func (x *xxhashReadFrom) ReadFrom(r io.Reader) (int64, error) {
   198	        for {
   199	                n, err := r.Read(x.buff)
   200	                if n > 0 {
   201	                        x.Digest.Write(x.buff[:n])
   202	                }
   203	                if err != nil {
   204	                        if err == io.EOF {
   205	                                err = nil
   206	                        }
   207	                        return int64(n), err
   208	                }
   209	        }
   210	}

   609	        r := rc.clone()
   610	
   611	        if u.content != nil {
   612	                r.sd.OpenReadSeekCloser = func() (hugio.ReadSeekCloser, error) {
   613	                        return hugio.NewReadSeekerNoOpCloserFromString(*u.content), nil
   614	                }
   615	        }
   616	
   617	        r.sd.MediaType = u.mediaType
   618	
   619	        if u.sourceFilename != nil {
   620	                if u.sourceFs == nil {
   621	                        return nil, errors.New("sourceFs is nil")
   622	                }
   623	                r.setOpenSource(func() (hugio.ReadSeekCloser, error) {
   624	                        return u.sourceFs.Open(*u.sourceFilename)
   625	                })
   626	        } else if u.sourceFs != nil {
   627	                return nil, errors.New("sourceFs is set without sourceFilename")
   628	        }
   629	
   630	        if u.targetPath == "" {
   631	                return nil, errors.New("missing targetPath")
   632	        }
   633	
   634	        r.setTargetPath(r.paths.FromTargetPath(u.targetPath))
   635	        r.mergeData(u.data)
   636	
   637	        return r, nil
   638	}
   639	
   640	func (l genericResource) clone() *genericResource {

   110	func NewReadSeekerNoOpCloserFromReader(r io.Reader) (readSeekerNopCloser, error) {
   111	        var rs io.ReadSeeker
   112	        if s, ok := r.(io.ReadSeeker); ok {
   113	                rs = s
   114	        } else {
   115	                b, err := io.ReadAll(r)
   116	                if err != nil {
   117	                        return readSeekerNopCloser{rs}, err
   118	                }
   119	                rs = bytes.NewReader(b)
   120	        }
   121	        return readSeekerNopCloser{rs}, nil
   122	}
   123	
   124	// NewOpenReadSeekCloser creates a new ReadSeekCloser from the given ReadSeeker.
   125	// The ReadSeeker will be seeked to the beginning before returned.
   126	func NewOpenReadSeekCloser(r ReadSeekCloser) OpenReadSeekCloser {
   127	        return func() (ReadSeekCloser, error) {
   128	                r.Seek(0, io.SeekStart)
   129	                return r, nil
   130	        }
   131	}

cat >/tmp/repro_addresource_shared_reader.go <<'EOF'
package main

import (
    "fmt"
    "io"
    "strings"
    "sync"

    "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/resources/page/pagemeta"
)

type slowReader struct {
    r io.Reader
    started chan struct{}
    proceed chan struct{}
    once sync.Once
}

func (s *slowReader) Read(p []byte) (int, error) {
    if len(p) > 8 { p = p[:8] }
    n, err := s.r.Read(p)
    s.once.Do(func(){ close(s.started); <-s.proceed })
    return n, err
}

func main() {
    content := strings.Repeat("abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz", 10000)
    open := (pagemeta.Source{Value: content}).ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser()

    r1, err := open()
    if err != nil { panic(err) }
    sr := &slowReader{r: r1, started: make(chan struct{}), proceed: make(chan struct{})}
    var got1 string
    var wg sync.WaitGroup
    wg.Add(1)
    go func() {
        defer wg.Done()
        b, err := io.ReadAll(sr)
        if err != nil { panic(err) }
        got1 = string(b)
    }()
    <-sr.started

    r2, err := open() // seeks the same underlying reader back to offset 0 while r1 is still in use.
    if err != nil { panic(err) }
    if _, err := io.ReadAll(r2); err != nil { panic(err) }
    close(sr.proceed)
    wg.Wait()

    if got1 != content {
        fmt.Printf("reproduced shared reader corruption: got len %d, want %d\n", len(got1), len(content))
        return
    }
    panic("did not reproduce")
}
EOF

cat >/tmp/repro_addresource_shared_reader.go <<'EOF'
package main

import (
    "fmt"
    "io"
    "strings"
    "sync"

    "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/resources/page/pagemeta"
)

type slowReader struct {
    r       io.Reader
    started chan struct{}
    proceed chan struct{}
    once    sync.Once
}

func (s *slowReader) Read(p []byte) (int, error) {
    if len(p) > 8 {
        p = p[:8]
    }
    n, err := s.r.Read(p)
    s.once.Do(func() { close(s.started); <-s.proceed })
    return n, err
}

func main() {
    content := strings.Repeat("abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz", 10000)
    open := (pagemeta.Source{Value: content}).ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser()

    r1, err := open()
    if err != nil {
        panic(err)
    }
    sr := &slowReader{r: r1, started: make(chan struct{}), proceed: make(chan struct{})}
    var got1 string
    var wg sync.WaitGroup
    wg.Add(1)
    go func() {
        defer wg.Done()
        b, err := io.ReadAll(sr)
        if err != nil {
            panic(err)
        }
        got1 = string(b)
    }()
    <-sr.started

    r2, err := open()
    if err != nil {
        panic(err)
    }
    if _, err := io.ReadAll(r2); err != nil {
        panic(err)
    }
    close(sr.proceed)
    wg.Wait()

    if got1 != content {
        panic(fmt.Sprintf("shared reader corruption: got len %d, want %d", len(got1), len(content)))
    }
    fmt.Println("ok")
}
EOF
